On the left is a bedroom with a king bed and access to the second bath.  Past this to the right is an entrance to the master bedroom which also has full wall length folding doors which open for those amazing ocean views.   The master bedroom has a new  custom parota wood bedroom suit.  The master bedroom has a beautiful newly remodeled en suite bath with a large shower and plentiful storage.   Across the hallway from the master bedroom door is a large secondary bath which is also recently beautifully remodeled.  At the end of the entry hall you find the kitchen and main living area.   The area is an open concept to make the most of the beautiful views.   The kitchen is complete with gas range and stove, a large side by side refrigerator with filtered water dispenser and icemaker, a dishwasher, vent hood, and natural wood custom cabinetry.  The kitchen is well stocked with everything you need to prepare gourmet meals.  The living area has a large glass top parota dining table with 6 chairs.  There is a large couch, single chair, and  matching parota side tables and coffee table.   There is a window seat to take in views.   The Roku smart TV is connected to wifi and you can watch 1,000s of shows or movies with the installed app, or sign in to your Netflix account. There is a secondary sitting area with full length folding doors that open the home up to the outside with a metal railing.  Here you will spend hours watching the dolphins and whales play in the bay, and take in the most magnificent sunsets. There is a separate lockable private bodega with your own washer dryer across the breezeway from the front door.\u003cbr />\u003cbr />\u003cb>Guest access\u003c/b>\u003cbr />Our condominium offers access to incredible facilities. The building features a large heated pool where you can relax and cool off as well as a large kiddie pool.  There is a private beach area with palapas and chairs available for guests as well as a private lawn area and gardens.   A patio with a charcoal grill and gas grill is available for use by making a reservation with the office.   The condo itself is on the third floor.  An elevator is available as well as stairs from the building lobby.   A small library is available in the lobby area for guests to use.   There is a parking area in front of the building with spaces along the entrance drive as well.   Our complex and the adjacent complex are accessed by a security gate with guard.  There will be a code to enter the building and a code to enter the condo.\u003cbr />\u003cbr />**Please note that, according to the building regulations, the maximum occupancy allowed is 6 adults and 2 children under 13 years old.**\u003cbr />\u003cbr />\u003cb>Other things to note\u003c/b>\u003cbr />**Discounts offered for weekly and monthly rentals**\u003cbr />\u003cbr />The property will be cleaned with approved disinfectant that includes all touch-points such as: door knobs, counters, toilets, showers, tables and handrails. Upon check-in, guests will also be provided with a wristband, which must be worn during their stay. The rock piles along the beach make for some excellent snorkeling as the water at our beach is some of the clearest in all of Banderas Bay.
